           <div class="Pos-r sticky-container print-article" style="min-height:315px;">
            <div class="article-inner-container" style="max-width:1280px;">
             <div class="inset-container Mx-a">
              <div class="GridTable">
               <div class="D-tbr row-template">
                <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left">
                 <div class="content" style="width:825px;min-width:825px;">
                  <noscript>
                  </noscript>
                  <noscript>
                  </noscript>
                  <div class="GridTable grid-content">
                   <div class="D-tbr row-content">
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-left Pend-20" style="width:305px;max-width:305px;">
                     <h1 class="Font-A-6-110 title W-100" id="article-aft-title-96573345003">
                      Cant Touch Your Toes? Do This
                     </h1>
                     <div class="attribution-component D-b W-100" id="article-aft-attribution-96573345003" style="max-width:305px;">
                      <div class="author-info author-info-text-first Pt-10 W-100 Bd-t Bd-b Bdstart-0 Bdend-0">
                       <div class="GridTable W-100">
                        <div class="D-tbr">
                         <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t">
                          <cite class="byline col D-b Fs-n" style="padding-bottom:15px;">
                           <span class="author-name Font-C-2-140 D-b">
                            <a class="attribution-name Font-C-2-140 Fw-b Whs-n" data-ylk="t1:a2;t2:article;t3:cat;t8:38ba0d4c-fe5d-3e8d-bf5f-2e00f96c553a;t9:17;elm:itm;elmt:link;itc:0" href="https://twitter.com/xenstrengthyoga" style="color:#000;" target="_blank">
                             Danielle Diamond
                            </a>
                           </span>
                           <time class="date Font-C-2-140 Fw-n D-b">
                            <span>
                             September 4, 2014
                            </span>
                           </time>
                          </cite>
                         </div>
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="GridTable-Cell Va-t col-right" style="max-width:500px;">
                     <div class="text-body-wrapper W-100 Font-B-1-160">
                      <noscript>
                      </noscript>
                      <div class="text-body W-100 Font-B-1-160" id="article-aft-text-body-96573345003" style="color:#222222;max-width:500px;">
                       <div class="body read-more-cut">
                        <div class="pre-cut" style="height:auto;margin-bottom:1.5em;">
                         <p>
                          <img alt="Cant Touch Your Toes? Do This" height="358" src="https://s.yimg.com/cd/resizer/2.0/FIT_TO_WIDTH-w500/769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg" width="500"/>
                          <em>
                           Photo: Leslie Lewis
                          </em>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Im a yoga teacher, so I hear, I cant do yoga, Im not flexible and I cant touch my toes! at least once a day. The thing is, thats why you should be doing it in the first place. Regardless of how far your fingers are from the floor right now, there are yoga poses that can help you increase your flexibility and stretch those muscles. With enough practice, youll be able to scoop up that golf ball or tie your shoes without crouching down or sitting.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Its all that sitting, by the way, thats shortening your hamstrings in the first place. Your muscles get tight from inactivity or improper stretching before your workout. The good news? All you need is a few minutes a week to stretch them out. A
                          <a data-ylk="elm:itm;elmt:link;t1:a2;t2:article;t3:body;t8:38ba0d4c-fe5d-3e8d-bf5f-2e00f96c553a;t9:18;itc:0" href="http://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/15705041" target="_blank">
                           study
                          </a>
                          by the Department of Human Performance and Exercise Science, which focused specifically on hamstring flexibility, found that just 30 seconds of stretching, done three times a week, successfully helped lengthen the hamstrings after just four weeks. You also need to think about your deep hip muscles and the muscles that run down your back. Here are three poses that will open up your hip, back, and hamstring muscles. Stay in each pose for 10 long breaths, inhaling until your upper chest expands, and exhaling until your belly contracts toward your spine.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Bound Angle
                           <br/>
                          </strong>
                          From a seated position, bring the soles of your feet together, letting your knees release toward the floor. Lift through the crown of your head, keeping the spine long, and gently fold forward, extending the sternum toward the front of the mat. Instead of letting the spine round, keep lengthening out in front of you as you open up the hips and lower back.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Reclining Big Toe Pose
                           <br/>
                          </strong>
                          Lie on your back with a yoga strap or a towel looped around the sole of your foot. Straighten the leg and reach the heel toward the ceiling as you press the front of your thigh away from you, and bring the toes toward you in the opposite direction. Dont allow the ankle to come too far forward of the hip, as you want to keep the hip grounded on the floor as you stretch the hips, thighs, hamstrings, and calves.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          <strong>
                           Standing Forward Fold
                           <br/>
                          </strong>
                          Stand with your back against a wall, take one step away and bring your feet together or hip distance apart. Put a slight bend at your knees and hinge at your hips. Place your palms on your shins and fold forward as you begin to bring the crown of your head toward the center of the room. If you dont feel a stretch here, continue to fold deeper bringing the crown of your head toward the floor, bending the elbows if necessary. Eventually, you will be able to reach your fingers toward the floor or on yoga blocks to stretching out your hips, calves, hamstrings, and thighs in this pose.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Four weeks from now, youll officially be one of the flexible ones.
                         </p>
                        </div>
                        <div class="post-cut W-100" id="post-cut" style="transition-property:none;-webkit-transition-property:none;transition-duration:10s;-webkit-transition-duration:10s;transition-timing-function:ease-in;-webkit-transition-timing-function:ease-in;overflow:hidden;max-height:999999px;max-width:500px;">
                        </div>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </div>

According to Mallett, French women believe that shampooing frequently strips their hair of moisture. &#x201C;They&#x2019;re also less sporty than American women,&#x201D; he explains. &#x201C;I don&#x2019;t get many clients who need to shower after the gym.&#x201D; \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-shampoo-no-1\"\u003EL&#x2019;Hydratation shampoo\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($45) is ideal for color-treated or damaged hair because it hydrates without weight. It&#x2019;s low lathering, which means you need to do two applications with each wash. &#x201C;I like to use it as body wash,&#x201D; Mallett adds. In addition to the shampoo and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-conditioner-no-1\"\u003Econditioner\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($50), there is a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-mask-no-1\"\u003Ecreamy mask\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($75) for extremely dry hair. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EGet volume from products, not blowouts.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003ENo French woman wants to sacrifice volume for hydration,&#x201D; Mallett says. His second hair care range, No.2 Le Volume, made with Japanese nori seaweed protein, is specifically made for women with fine hair. &#x201C;The \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-shampoo-no-2\"\u003Eshampoo\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($45) takes some acclimation,&#x201D; he warns. &#x201C;When your hair is wet, it feels reinforced, but when it dries, it will be so much more voluminous.&#x201D; Instead of a conditioner, the line includes a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-spray-no-2\"\u003Evolumizing spray\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($40). &#x201C;Some French women don&#x2019;t even use conditioner because they wash so infrequently,&#x201D; he explains.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EFake effortless hair by getting your blowout the day before the big event.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E&#x201C;French women will just sleep on it,&#x201D; Mallett explains. The Australian hairstylist, originally from Perth, brought soft pink salt from Australia&#x2019;s Murray River to Paris for the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-australian-salt-spray\"\u003Esalt spray\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($40) he developed. &#x201C;Raw material from Australia, mixed in Paris &#x2014; just like me,&#x201D; he says. Unlike most salt sprays, Mallett&#x2019;s version doesn&#x2019;t smell like Coppertone or coconut. &#x201C;French girls don&#x2019;t relate to Hawaii,&#x201D; he explains. &#x201C;They relate more to the Mediterranean.&#x201D; This salt spray smells like Bergamot, a citrus fruit cultivated in Italy. He also developed a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair-serum\"\u003Eserum\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($80), made of nourishing macadamia nut oil, which is applied to wet hair and will keep your hair shinier for longer. &#x201C;French women will put in so much effort to look like they didn&#x2019;t do much at all,&#x201D; Mallett admits.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMani-pedis are a must, no matter how low-maintenance you seem.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003EAt Mallett&#x2019;s salon in Paris, both men and women get their manicures done by his in-demand technician, Laurence, who travels regularly with Karl Lagerfeld. &#x201C;In fact, only 40% of my female clients get manicures, while 90% of my male clients get manicures,&#x201D; he says. &#x201C;Men just don&#x2019;t own up to it.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"395\" height=\"266\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w395\u002Fbe50dd64b196189a4830beb8531b18e3e0ffbd93.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EDavid Mallett Beard Balm. (Photo: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-beard-balm\"\u003EShen Beauty\u003C\u002Fa\u003E)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMen, feel free to grow out your hair.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E&#x201C;Right now, French men are growing out their hair and beards,&#x201D; Mallett explains. &#x201C;No sharp ends.&#x201D; He developed a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.shen-beauty.com\u002Fcollections\u002Fdavid-mallet-hair\u002Fproducts\u002Fdavid-mallet-beard-balm\"\u003EBeard Balm\u003C\u002Fa\u003E ($35) that gives structure to the favored unruly facial hair he sees in his salon. Brands Need to Create More Color Options for Tinted Sunscreens","summary":"Tinted sunscreens dont seem to work for all skin types. Recently, the topic turned to tinted moisturizers, and the fact they often come in just one shade&#x2014;one that is somehow supposed to blend seamlessly into all skin tones (which seems totally impossible). So with my colleague Alais Diop and I working as guinea pigs, we decided to test them out. We tried out seven different brands, on my fair skin and her darker skin, to see if the products did indeed work with different skin colors. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOf the seven brands we tested, I found two that worked with my fair skin, while Alais only found one. Surprisingly, only two of the brands we tested &#x2014; Clarins and Shiseido &#x2014; offered tinted sunscreens in multiple shades. However, those brands only offered three options: Light, medium, and deep. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EGiven that the beauty business is global, we thought it was disappointing that more brands don&#x2019;t offer more color options for tinted sunscreens. While brands offer a vast color range when it comes to BB creams and tinted moisturizers, those products don&#x2019;t stack up when it comes to serious sun protection. &#x201C;I find that many tinted moisturizers and BB creams don&#x2019;t offer the same level of protection that a more traditional sunscreen has,&#x201D; says dermatologist Dr. Sejal Shah. &#x201C;Either they are not broad spectrum or the SPF tends to be lower. A tinted moisturizer or BB cream may be OK for daily use, but if you&#x2019;re going to be spending time outside then you really need to use a true sunscreen, and a tinted one can provide excellent protection while giving you the color coverage you desire.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHere&#x2019;s hoping that the beauty brands start expanding their color ranges. Do This","summary":"Photo: Leslie Lewis Im a yoga teacher, so I hear, I cant do yoga, Im not flexible and I cant touch my toes! at least once a day.  Its all that sitting, by the way, thats shortening your hamstrings in the first place.  A study by the Department of Human Performance and Exercise Science, which focused specifically on hamstring flexibility, found that just 30 seconds of stretching, done three times a week, successfully helped lengthen the hamstrings after just four weeks.  You also need to think about your deep hip muscles and the muscles that run down your back.","body":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w500\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg\" width=\"500\" height=\"358\" alt=\"Can&#x2019;t Touch Your Toes? Do This\"\u003E\u003Cem\u003EPhoto: Leslie Lewis\u003C\u002Fem\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EI&#x2019;m a yoga teacher, so I hear, &#x201C;I can&#x2019;t do yoga, I&#x2019;m not flexible and I can&#x2019;t touch my toes!&#x201D; at least once a day. The thing is, that&#x2019;s why you should be doing it in the first place. Regardless of how far your fingers are from the floor right now, there are yoga poses that can help you increase your flexibility and stretch those muscles. With enough practice, you&#x2019;ll be able to scoop up that golf ball or tie your shoes without crouching down or sitting.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIt&#x2019;s all that sitting, by the way, that&#x2019;s shortening your hamstrings in the first place. Your muscles get tight from inactivity or improper stretching before your workout. The good news? All you need is a few minutes a week to stretch them out. A \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\u002Fpubmed\u002F15705041\"\u003Estudy\u003C\u002Fa\u003E by the Department of Human Performance and Exercise Science, which focused specifically on hamstring flexibility, found that just 30 seconds of stretching, done three times a week, successfully helped lengthen the hamstrings after just four weeks. You also need to think about your deep hip muscles and the muscles that run down your back. Here are three poses that will open up your hip, back, and hamstring muscles. Stay in each pose for 10 long breaths, inhaling until your upper chest expands, and exhaling until your belly contracts toward your spine.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EBound Angle\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003EFrom a seated position, bring the soles of your feet together, letting your knees release toward the floor. Lift through the crown of your head, keeping the spine long, and gently fold forward, extending the sternum toward the front of the mat. Instead of letting the spine round, keep lengthening out in front of you as you open up the hips and lower back.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EReclining Big Toe Pose\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003ELie on your back with a yoga strap or a towel looped around the sole of your foot.&#xA0; Straighten the leg and reach the heel toward the ceiling as you press the front of your thigh away from you, and bring the toes toward you in the opposite direction. Don&#x2019;t allow the ankle to come too far forward of the hip, as you want to keep the hip grounded on the floor as you stretch the hips, thighs, hamstrings, and calves.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EStanding Forward Fold\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003EStand with your back against a wall, take one step away and bring your feet together or hip distance apart. Put a slight bend at your knees and hinge at your hips. Place your palms on your shins and fold forward as you begin to bring the crown of your head toward the center of the room. If you don&#x2019;t feel a stretch here, continue to fold deeper bringing the crown of your head toward the floor, bending the elbows if necessary. Eventually, you will be able to reach your fingers toward the floor or on yoga blocks to stretching out your hips, calves, hamstrings, and thighs in this pose.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EFour weeks from now, you&#x2019;ll officially be one of the flexible ones.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E","content_status":"UNPUBLISHED","td_applet_infos":[],"canonical_urls":[],"uploaded_images":[],"type":"story","wiki_ids":[],"yct_categories":["yct:001000506"],"privateTags":[],"leadImages":[{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w175\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":175,"height":125,"size_type":"175","formats":{},"types":{"image\u002Fjpeg":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w175\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg"}},{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w200\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":200,"height":143,"size_type":"200","formats":{},"types":{"image\u002Fjpeg":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w200\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg"}},{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w250\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":250,"height":179,"size_type":"250","formats":{},"types":{"image\u002Fjpeg":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w250\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg"}},{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w300\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":300,"height":215,"size_type":"300","formats":{},"types":{"image\u002Fjpeg":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w300\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg"}},{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w350\u002F769c493ab1bdb87ae15fd59c5d5d56afb5b1a904.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":350,"height":251,"size_type":"350","formats":{},"types":{"image\u002Fjpe
